How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

Loot Chart

#1

- Gear: Lantern
- Rarity: Epic
- Gear Type: One-Handed Weapon
- Color: Gray
- Weapon Damage: d8 AOE Ranged
- Stat Buffs
    - Damage Plus ✦ = L
    - Attack Plus ✦ = L
    - Perception ✦ = Lx1.25
    - Intelligence = D
- Actives:
    - [Empowered AOE Attack](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Empowered+AOE+Attack)
    - [Gray Combo Attack](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Gray+Combo+Attack)
    - You have access to Tiers I-III of each of your Actives.
- Essence Value: 5000
- Credit Value: 500
- Aesthetic: Rtolkan (Steampunk)
